(@p292, @p293, @p294, @p295, 73),
(@p296, @p297, @p298, @p299, 74),
(@p300, @p301, @p302, @p303, 75),
(@p304, @p305, @p306, @p307, 76),
(@p308, @p309, @p310, @p311, 77)) AS i ([AccuWeatherLocalizationKey], [CityName], [Latitude], [Longitude], _Position) ON 1=0
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
INSERT ([AccuWeatherLocalizationKey], [CityName], [Latitude], [Longitude])
VALUES (i.[AccuWeatherLocalizationKey], i.[CityName], i.[Latitude], i.[Longitude])
OUTPUT INSERTED.[Id], i._Position
INTO @inserted0;

SELECT [t].[Id] FROM [BigCitiesData] t
INNER JOIN @inserted0 i ON ([t].[Id] = [i].[Id])
ORDER BY [i].[_Position];
